<h1 id="import-libraries">Import libraries</h1>
<p>This notebook requires matplotlib for plotting, NumPy for numerical operations, and SciPy for nonlinear data-fitting. The time and datetime modules are included only for timing the execution of the fitting operation.</p>
</div>
<div class="cell border-box-sizing code_cell vbox">
<div class="input hbox">
<div class="prompt input_prompt">
In&nbsp;[1]:
</div>
<div class="input_area box-flex1">
<div class="highlight"><pre><span class="kn">import</span> <span class="nn">matplotlib.pyplot</span> <span class="kn">as</span> <span class="nn">plt</span>
<span class="kn">import</span> <span class="nn">numpy</span> <span class="kn">as</span> <span class="nn">np</span>
<span class="kn">import</span> <span class="nn">scipy.optimize</span> <span class="kn">as</span> <span class="nn">opt</span>
<span class="kn">import</span> <span class="nn">collections</span>
<span class="kn">from</span> <span class="nn">scipy.integrate</span> <span class="kn">import</span> <span class="n">odeint</span>
<span class="kn">import</span> <span class="nn">time</span>
<span class="kn">import</span> <span class="nn">datetime</span>

</pre></div>

<div class="text_cell_render border-box-sizing rendered_html">
<h1 id="read-the-data-files.">Read the data files.</h1>
<p>The data files I received contained the ionic current, and the integrated gating current (i.e, the gating charge).</p>
<p>To recover the gating current, we have to take the derivative of the gating charge.</p>
</div>
<div class="cell border-box-sizing code_cell vbox">
<div class="input hbox">
<div class="prompt input_prompt">
In&nbsp;[2]:
</div>
<div class="input_area box-flex1">
<div class="highlight"><pre><span class="c"># Manually generate variable potential sweep</span>
<span class="n">gv</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="p">[</span><span class="o">-</span><span class="mi">100</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="o">-</span><span class="mi">90</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="o">-</span><span class="mi">80</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="o">-</span><span class="mi">70</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="o">-</span><span class="mi">60</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="o">-</span><span class="mi">50</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="o">-</span><span class="mi">40</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="o">-</span><span class="mi">30</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="o">-</span><span class="mi">20</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="o">-</span><span class="mi">10</span><span class="p">]</span>

<span class="c"># Manually generate time course data</span>
<span class="n">dt</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="mf">0.00006</span>
<span class="n">t</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">np</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">arange</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="mf">0.3</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">dt</span><span class="p">)</span>

<span class="c"># Read in the data files (use PANDAS instead?)</span>
<span class="n">gi</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">np</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">genfromtxt</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s">&#39;gi.txt&#39;</span><span class="p">)</span>
<span class="n">ii</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">np</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">genfromtxt</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s">&#39;ii.txt&#39;</span><span class="p">)</span>

<span class="c"># Normalize ionic current</span>
<span class="n">ii</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">ii</span> <span class="o">/</span> <span class="n">np</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">max</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">ii</span><span class="p">)</span>

<span class="c"># Normalize gating charge</span>
<span class="n">gc</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">gi</span> <span class="o">/</span> <span class="n">np</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">max</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">gi</span><span class="p">)</span>

<span class="c"># Take the gradient of the integrated sweeps to recover current</span>
<span class="n">gi</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">np</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">gradient</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">gi</span><span class="p">)[</span><span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="o">/</span> <span class="n">np</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">max</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">np</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">gradient</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">gi</span><span class="p">)[</span><span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">])</span>

<span class="c"># Neglect the first few points and last few points</span>
<span class="n">gc</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">gc</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="mi">10</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="o">-</span><span class="mi">40</span><span class="p">]</span>
<span class="n">gi</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">gi</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="mi">10</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="o">-</span><span class="mi">40</span><span class="p">]</span>
<span class="n">ii</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">ii</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="mi">10</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="o">-</span><span class="mi">40</span><span class="p">]</span>
<span class="n">t</span>  <span class="o">=</span>  <span class="n">t</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="mi">10</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="o">-</span><span class="mi">40</span><span class="p">]</span>

<span class="k">def</span> <span class="nf">plotall</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">i</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">g</span><span class="p">):</span>
    <span class="n">plt</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">figure</span><span class="p">()</span>
    <span class="n">plt</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">title</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s">&#39;Ionic Current&#39;</span><span class="p">)</span>
    <span class="n">plt</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">plot</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">i</span><span class="p">)</span>

    <span class="n">plt</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">figure</span><span class="p">()</span>
    <span class="n">plt</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">title</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s">&#39;Gating Current&#39;</span><span class="p">)</span>
    <span class="n">plt</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">plot</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">g</span><span class="p">)</span>
    <span class="k">return</span>

<span class="c"># Show data</span>
<span class="n">plotall</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">ii</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">gi</span><span class="p">)</span>
</pre></div>

</div>

<h1 id="define-the-markov-system">Define the Markov System</h1>
<p>Here we use a modified Hodgkin-Huxley model to fit the data. We assume there are four closed states (the last two with partial conductance), an open conducting state, and an inactivated state.</p>
$ C_0

C_1

C_2

C_3

C_4

Op

<p>I $</p>
<p>The forward and backward voltage-dependent kinetic rates can be described by the following formula:</p>
$

<p>$</p>
<p>Before each experimental trace, the membrane is held at a negative &quot;hyperpolarized&quot; potential for an extended period of time until the system reaches equilibrium. We can impose this initial condition by noting that it is in steady state, and therefore <span class="math">\(\frac{d C_0}{dt} = 0\)</span></p>
</div>
<div class="cell border-box-sizing code_cell vbox">
<div class="input hbox">
<div class="prompt input_prompt">
In&nbsp;[3]:
</div>
<div class="input_area box-flex1">
<div class="highlight"><pre><span class="c"># Rate parameters - memb potential in mV</span>
<span class="k">def</span> <span class="nf">rate</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">c</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">z</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">mV</span><span class="p">):</span>

    <span class="n">kB</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="mf">0.086173</span><span class="p">;</span> <span class="c"># in e mV/K</span>
    <span class="n">T</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="mi">300</span><span class="p">;</span> <span class="c"># in K</span>
 
    <span class="n">rate</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">c</span> <span class="o">*</span> <span class="n">np</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">exp</span><span class="p">(</span> <span class="n">z</span> <span class="o">*</span> <span class="n">mV</span> <span class="o">/</span> <span class="n">kB</span> <span class="o">/</span> <span class="n">T</span> <span class="p">)</span>
    <span class="k">return</span> <span class="n">rate</span>


<span class="c"># Define the system</span>
<span class="c">#</span>
<span class="c">#        4a        3a        2a        1a       kco</span>
<span class="c">#   C0 &lt;====&gt; C1 &lt;====&gt; C2 &lt;====&gt; C3 &lt;====&gt; C4 &lt;===&gt; Op</span>
<span class="c">#        1b        2b        3b        4b       koc</span>
<span class="c">#</span>
<span class="c">#</span>

<span class="k">def</span> <span class="nf">Mat</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">prm</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">V</span><span class="p">):</span>
    <span class="n">prm</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">np</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">abs</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">prm</span><span class="p">)</span>
    <span class="n">c1</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">c2</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">zf</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">zb</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">kco</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">koc</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">kio</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">koi</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">Gm1</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">Gm2</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">Gm3</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">Gm4</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">prm</span>    
    <span class="n">a</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">rate</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">c1</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">zf</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">V</span><span class="p">)</span>
    <span class="n">b</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">rate</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">c2</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="o">-</span><span class="n">zb</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">V</span><span class="p">)</span>

    <span class="n">M</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="p">[[</span><span class="o">-</span><span class="mi">4</span><span class="o">*</span><span class="n">a</span><span class="p">,</span>      <span class="n">b</span><span class="p">,</span>        <span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">,</span>      <span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">,</span>        <span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">,</span>        <span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">,</span>    <span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">],</span>
         <span class="p">[</span> <span class="mi">4</span><span class="o">*</span><span class="n">a</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="o">-</span><span class="n">b</span><span class="o">-</span><span class="mi">3</span><span class="o">*</span><span class="n">a</span><span class="p">,</span>      <span class="mi">2</span><span class="o">*</span><span class="n">b</span><span class="p">,</span>      <span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">,</span>        <span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">,</span>        <span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">,</span>    <span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">],</span>
         <span class="p">[</span>   <span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">,</span>    <span class="mi">3</span><span class="o">*</span><span class="n">a</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="o">-</span><span class="mi">2</span><span class="o">*</span><span class="n">b</span><span class="o">-</span><span class="mi">2</span><span class="o">*</span><span class="n">a</span><span class="p">,</span>    <span class="mi">3</span><span class="o">*</span><span class="n">b</span><span class="p">,</span>        <span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">,</span>        <span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">,</span>    <span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">],</span>
         <span class="p">[</span>   <span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">,</span>      <span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">,</span>      <span class="mi">2</span><span class="o">*</span><span class="n">a</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="o">-</span><span class="mi">3</span><span class="o">*</span><span class="n">b</span><span class="o">-</span><span class="n">a</span><span class="p">,</span>      <span class="mi">4</span><span class="o">*</span><span class="n">b</span><span class="p">,</span>        <span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">,</span>    <span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">],</span>
         <span class="p">[</span>   <span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">,</span>      <span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">,</span>        <span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">,</span>      <span class="n">a</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="o">-</span><span class="mi">4</span><span class="o">*</span><span class="n">b</span><span class="o">-</span><span class="n">kco</span><span class="p">,</span>      <span class="n">koc</span><span class="p">,</span>    <span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">],</span>
         <span class="p">[</span>   <span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">,</span>      <span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">,</span>        <span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">,</span>      <span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">,</span>      <span class="n">kco</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="o">-</span><span class="n">koc</span><span class="o">-</span><span class="n">koi</span><span class="p">,</span>  <span class="n">kio</span><span class="p">],</span>
         <span class="p">[</span>   <span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">,</span>      <span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">,</span>        <span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">,</span>      <span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">,</span>        <span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">,</span>      <span class="n">koi</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="o">-</span><span class="n">kio</span><span class="p">]]</span>

    <span class="k">return</span> <span class="n">M</span>


<span class="k">def</span> <span class="nf">f</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">y</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">t</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">prm</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">V</span><span class="p">):</span>
    <span class="c"># This function defines the system of ordinary differential equations (ODE)</span>
    <span class="c">#C0, C1, C2, C3, C4, Op, I = y</span>
    
    <span class="c"># Matrix is unique at every voltage</span>
    <span class="n">M</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">Mat</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">prm</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">V</span><span class="p">)</span>

    <span class="c"># This represents the system of equations, where y_prime is the rate of change of each state</span>
    <span class="n">y_prime</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">np</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">dot</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">M</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="n">y</span><span class="p">)</span>

    <span class="k">return</span> <span class="n">y_prime</span>


<span class="k">def</span> <span class="nf">ybaseline</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">prm</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">Vholding</span><span class="p">):</span>
    <span class="c"># For given set of parameters, find the steady state condition</span>
    <span class="c"># i.e. Mx=0, and sum x = 1</span>

    <span class="n">m</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">Mat</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">prm</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">Vholding</span><span class="p">)</span>

    <span class="c"># Add an extra row for steady state condition</span>
    <span class="n">M</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">np</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">vstack</span><span class="p">((</span><span class="n">m</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">np</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">ones</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="nb">len</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">m</span><span class="p">))))</span>

    <span class="c"># Find initial populations which satisfy steady state condition</span>
    <span class="n">ybsl</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">residuals</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">rank</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">s</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">np</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">linalg</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">lstsq</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">M</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="p">[</span><span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">])</span>
    
    <span class="k">return</span> <span class="n">ybsl</span>
    
<span class="c"># Just for testing --- do not use</span>
<span class="c">#f([1,0,0,0,0,0,0], t, Pini, 88)</span>
<span class="c">#ybaseline(Pini, -88)</span>
</pre></div>

<span class="n">prms</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="p">((</span><span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">,</span>  <span class="s">&#39;c1&#39;</span><span class="p">,</span>     <span class="mi">10</span><span class="p">,</span>       <span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">,</span>  <span class="mf">1e4</span><span class="p">),</span>

        <span class="p">(</span><span class="mi">3</span><span class="p">,</span>  <span class="s">&#39;zb&#39;</span><span class="p">,</span>      <span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">,</span>       <span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">,</span>    <span class="mi">2</span><span class="p">),</span>
        <span class="p">(</span><span class="mi">4</span><span class="p">,</span>  <span class="s">&#39;kco&#39;</span><span class="p">,</span>     <span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">,</span>       <span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">,</span>  <span class="mf">1e4</span><span class="p">),</span>
        <span class="p">(</span><span class="mi">5</span><span class="p">,</span>  <span class="s">&#39;koc&#39;</span><span class="p">,</span>     <span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">,</span>       <span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">,</span>  <span class="mf">1e4</span><span class="p">),</span>

        <span class="p">(</span><span class="mi">7</span><span class="p">,</span>  <span class="s">&#39;koi&#39;</span><span class="p">,</span>     <span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">,</span>       <span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">,</span>    <span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">),</span>
        <span class="p">(</span><span class="mi">8</span><span class="p">,</span>  <span class="s">&#39;Gm1&#39;</span><span class="p">,</span>     <span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">,</span>       <span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">,</span>  <span class="mf">1e4</span><span class="p">),</span>
        <span class="p">(</span><span class="mi">9</span><span class="p">,</span>  <span class="s">&#39;Gm2&#39;</span><span class="p">,</span>     <span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">,</span>       <span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">,</span>  <span class="mf">1e4</span><span class="p">),</span>
        <span class="p">(</span><span class="mi">10</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="s">&#39;Gm3&#39;</span><span class="p">,</span>     <span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">,</span>       <span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">,</span>    <span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">),</span>
        <span class="p">(</span><span class="mi">11</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="s">&#39;Gm4&#39;</span><span class="p">,</span>     <span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">,</span>       <span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">,</span>    <span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">))</span>


<span class="c"># convert named tuple to two lists: pinit and bounds</span>
<span class="k">def</span> <span class="nf">getprms</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">prms</span><span class="p">):</span>
    <span class="n">Pinit</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="n">np</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">zeros</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="nb">len</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">prms</span><span class="p">))</span>
    <span class="n">BndLo</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="n">np</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">zeros</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="nb">len</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">prms</span><span class="p">))</span>
    <span class="n">BndHi</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="n">np</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">zeros</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="nb">len</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">prms</span><span class="p">))</span>

    <span class="k">for</span> <span class="n">prm</span> <span class="ow">in</span> <span class="nb">map</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">Params</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">_make</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">prms</span><span class="p">):</span>
        <span class="c"># print &quot;%s %s %s&quot; % (p.index, p.name, p.value)</span>
        <span class="n">Pinit</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="n">prm</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">index</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">prm</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">value</span>
        <span class="n">BndLo</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="n">prm</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">index</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">prm</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">lo</span>
        <span class="n">BndHi</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="n">prm</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">index</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">prm</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">hi</span>
    
    <span class="n">Bounds</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="nb">zip</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">BndLo</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">BndHi</span><span class="p">)</span>
    <span class="k">return</span> <span class="n">Pinit</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">Bounds</span>


<span class="n">Pinit</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">Bounds</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">getprms</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">prms</span><span class="p">)</span>

<span class="c"># Assume the whole population start in C0 state</span>
<span class="n">C0i</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="mi">1</span>
<span class="n">C1i</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="mi">0</span>
<span class="n">C2i</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="mi">0</span>
<span class="n">C3i</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="mi">0</span>
<span class="n">C4i</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="mi">0</span>
<span class="n">Opi</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="mi">0</span>
<span class="n">Ii</span>  <span class="o">=</span> <span class="mi">0</span>

<span class="n">y0</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="p">[</span><span class="n">C0i</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">C1i</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">C2i</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">C3i</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">C4i</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">Opi</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">Ii</span><span class="p">]</span>
</pre></div>

</div>
</div>

</div>
<div class="text_cell_render border-box-sizing rendered_html">
<h1 id="evaluate-the-model">Evaluate the model</h1>
<p>The model can be evaluated by solving the equations and seeing if they fit the data. The set of differential equations produce a time-dependent population of states, which give rise to ionic and gating currents.</p>
</div>
<div class="cell border-box-sizing code_cell vbox">
<div class="input hbox">
<div class="prompt input_prompt">
In&nbsp;[5]:
</div>
<div class="input_area box-flex1">
<div class="highlight"><pre><span class="k">def</span> <span class="nf">evalmod</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">f</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">y0</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">t</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">prm</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">mV</span><span class="p">):</span>

    <span class="n">prm</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">np</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">abs</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">prm</span><span class="p">)</span>
    <span class="n">c1</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">c2</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">zf</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">zb</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">kco</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">koc</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">kio</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">koi</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">Gm1</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">Gm2</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">Gm3</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">Gm4</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">prm</span>
    <span class="n">a</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">rate</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">c1</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">zf</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">mV</span><span class="p">)</span>
    <span class="n">b</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">rate</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">c2</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="o">-</span><span class="n">zb</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">mV</span><span class="p">)</span>

    <span class="c">#solve the system of ODE</span>
    <span class="n">soln</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">odeint</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">f</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">y0</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">t</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">args</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">prm</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="n">mV</span><span class="p">))</span>

    <span class="c">#these are the solved traces for each state    C0t = soln[:,0]</span>
    <span class="n">C0t</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">soln</span><span class="p">[:,</span><span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">]</span>
    <span class="n">C1t</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">soln</span><span class="p">[:,</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">]</span>
    <span class="n">C2t</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">soln</span><span class="p">[:,</span><span class="mi">2</span><span class="p">]</span>
    <span class="n">C3t</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">soln</span><span class="p">[:,</span><span class="mi">3</span><span class="p">]</span>
    <span class="n">C4t</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">soln</span><span class="p">[:,</span><span class="mi">4</span><span class="p">]</span>
    <span class="n">Opt</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">soln</span><span class="p">[:,</span><span class="mi">5</span><span class="p">]</span>
    <span class="n">It</span>  <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">soln</span><span class="p">[:,</span><span class="mi">6</span><span class="p">]</span>

    <span class="c"># Ek is reversal potential </span>
    <span class="n">Ek</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="o">-</span><span class="mi">88</span>
    <span class="n">ionic</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">Gm1</span> <span class="o">*</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="n">mV</span> <span class="o">-</span> <span class="n">Ek</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="o">*</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="n">Opt</span> <span class="o">+</span> <span class="n">Gm3</span> <span class="o">*</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="n">C4t</span> <span class="o">+</span> <span class="n">Gm4</span> <span class="o">*</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="n">C3t</span> <span class="o">+</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="mi">0</span> <span class="o">*</span> <span class="n">C2t</span><span class="p">))))</span>

    <span class="c">#gating current</span>
    <span class="n">C0C1</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="mi">4</span><span class="o">*</span><span class="n">a</span><span class="o">*</span><span class="n">C0t</span> <span class="o">-</span> <span class="mi">1</span><span class="o">*</span><span class="n">b</span><span class="o">*</span><span class="n">C1t</span><span class="p">)</span>
    <span class="n">C1C2</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="mi">3</span><span class="o">*</span><span class="n">a</span><span class="o">*</span><span class="n">C1t</span> <span class="o">-</span> <span class="mi">2</span><span class="o">*</span><span class="n">b</span><span class="o">*</span><span class="n">C2t</span><span class="p">)</span>
    <span class="n">C2C3</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="mi">2</span><span class="o">*</span><span class="n">a</span><span class="o">*</span><span class="n">C2t</span> <span class="o">-</span> <span class="mi">3</span><span class="o">*</span><span class="n">b</span><span class="o">*</span><span class="n">C3t</span><span class="p">)</span>
    <span class="n">C3C4</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="o">*</span><span class="n">a</span><span class="o">*</span><span class="n">C3t</span> <span class="o">-</span> <span class="mi">4</span><span class="o">*</span><span class="n">b</span><span class="o">*</span><span class="n">C4t</span><span class="p">)</span>
    <span class="n">gating</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">Gm2</span> <span class="o">*</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="n">zf</span> <span class="o">-</span> <span class="n">zb</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="o">*</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="n">C0C1</span> <span class="o">+</span> <span class="n">C1C2</span> <span class="o">+</span> <span class="n">C2C3</span> <span class="o">+</span> <span class="n">C3C4</span><span class="p">)</span>

    <span class="k">return</span> <span class="n">ionic</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">gating</span>


<span class="k">def</span> <span class="nf">evalmodgroup</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">f</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">y0</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">t</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">prm</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">gv</span><span class="p">):</span>
    <span class="n">ionic</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">np</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">zeros</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">np</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">shape</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">ii</span><span class="p">))</span>
    <span class="n">gating</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">np</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">zeros</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">np</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">shape</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">gi</span><span class="p">))</span>
    <span class="k">for</span> <span class="n">i</span> <span class="ow">in</span> <span class="n">np</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">arange</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="nb">len</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">gv</span><span class="p">)):</span>
        <span class="n">mp</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">gv</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="n">i</span><span class="p">]</span>
        <span class="n">ionic</span><span class="p">[:,</span><span class="n">i</span><span class="p">],</span> <span class="n">gating</span><span class="p">[:,</span><span class="n">i</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">evalmod</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">f</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">y0</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">t</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">prm</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">mp</span><span class="p">)</span>
    <span class="k">return</span> <span class="n">ionic</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">gating</span>


<span class="c"># Evaluate with initial parameters as a test</span>
<span class="n">testi</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">testg</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">evalmodgroup</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">f</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">y0</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">t</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">Pinit</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">gv</span><span class="p">)</span>
<span class="n">plotall</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">testi</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">testg</span><span class="p">)</span>
</pre></div>

<div class="text_cell_render border-box-sizing rendered_html">
<h1 id="define-the-objective-function">Define the objective function</h1>
<p>The objective function is (for now) just the residual error.</p>
</div>
<div class="cell border-box-sizing code_cell vbox">
<div class="input hbox">
<div class="prompt input_prompt">
In&nbsp;[6]:
</div>
<div class="input_area box-flex1">
<div class="highlight"><pre><span class="k">def</span> <span class="nf">residualerr2arr</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">prm</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">y0</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">ii</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">gi</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">gv</span><span class="p">):</span>

    <span class="n">sim_ionic</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">sim_gating</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">evalmodgroup</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">f</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">y0</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">t</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">prm</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">gv</span><span class="p">)</span>

    <span class="n">err2_ionic</span>  <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">np</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">square</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">ii</span> <span class="o">-</span> <span class="n">sim_ionic</span><span class="p">)</span>
    <span class="n">err2_gating</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">np</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">square</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">gi</span> <span class="o">-</span> <span class="n">sim_gating</span><span class="p">)</span>

    <span class="n">err2_arr</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">err2_ionic</span> <span class="o">+</span> <span class="n">err2_gating</span>
    <span class="k">return</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="n">np</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">sum</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">err2_arr</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">axis</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">))</span>

<span class="k">def</span> <span class="nf">residualerr2sum</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">prm</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">y0</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">ii</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">gi</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">gv</span><span class="p">):</span>
    <span class="n">err2_arr</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">residualerr2arr</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">prm</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">y0</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">ii</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">gi</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">gv</span><span class="p">)</span>
    <span class="k">return</span> <span class="n">np</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">sqrt</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">np</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">sum</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">err2_arr</span><span class="p">))</span>

<span class="c"># test if function works</span>
<span class="c">#print residualerr2arr(Pinit, y0, ii, gi, gv)</span>
<span class="c">#print residualerr2sum(Pinit, y0, ii, gi, gv)</span>
</pre></div>

</div>
</div>

</div>
<div class="text_cell_render border-box-sizing rendered_html">
<h1 id="assess">Assess</h1>
<p>Given a function and some parameters, I can calculate simulated data. Furthermore, given some experimental data, I can calculate residual error for assessing the quality of the parameters.</p>
</div>
<div class="cell border-box-sizing code_cell vbox">
<div class="input hbox">
<div class="prompt input_prompt">
In&nbsp;[10]:
</div>
<div class="input_area box-flex1">
<div class="highlight"><pre><span class="k">def</span> <span class="nf">assess</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">Pinit</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">y0</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">ii</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">gi</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">gv</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">iterations</span><span class="p">):</span>
    
    <span class="k">print</span> <span class="s">&quot;Initial parameters used for solver:&quot;</span>
    <span class="k">print</span> <span class="n">Pinit</span>
    <span class="k">print</span> <span class="s">&quot;Initial conditions used for solver&quot;</span>
    <span class="k">print</span> <span class="n">y0</span>
    <span class="k">print</span> <span class="s">&quot;&quot;</span>

    <span class="c"># Store the values at each iteration to see how they behave</span>
    <span class="n">output_prms</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">np</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">zeros</span><span class="p">((</span><span class="nb">len</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">Pinit</span><span class="p">),</span> <span class="n">iterations</span><span class="p">))</span>
    <span class="n">output_y0</span>   <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">np</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">zeros</span><span class="p">((</span><span class="nb">len</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">y0</span><span class="p">),</span> <span class="n">iterations</span><span class="p">))</span>

    <span class="c"># Start timer</span>
    <span class="n">tic</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">time</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">time</span><span class="p">()</span>
    
    <span class="k">for</span> <span class="n">i</span> <span class="ow">in</span> <span class="n">np</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">arange</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">iterations</span><span class="p">):</span>

        <span class="k">print</span> <span class="s">&quot;Iteration: </span><span class="si">%s</span><span class="s">/</span><span class="si">%s</span><span class="s">&quot;</span> <span class="o">%</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="n">i</span><span class="o">+</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">iterations</span><span class="p">)</span>
    
        <span class="c"># Save history of parameters and initial populations</span>
        <span class="n">output_prms</span><span class="p">[:,</span><span class="n">i</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">Pinit</span>
        <span class="n">output_y0</span><span class="p">[:,</span><span class="n">i</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">y0</span>
    
        <span class="c"># Sequential Least Squares Programming</span>
        <span class="n">slsqp</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">opt</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">minimize</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">residualerr2sum</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">Pinit</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">args</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">y0</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">ii</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">gi</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">gv</span><span class="p">),</span> 
                            <span class="n">method</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="s">&#39;SLSQP&#39;</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">bounds</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="n">Bounds</span><span class="p">)</span>

        <span class="c"># get best parameter solution</span>
        <span class="n">sol</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">slsqp</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">x</span>
    
        <span class="c"># find baseline y values --- should be at Vholding</span>
        <span class="n">ybl</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">ybaseline</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">sol</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="o">-</span><span class="mi">90</span><span class="p">)</span>
        <span class="n">ybl_half</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">np</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">average</span><span class="p">((</span><span class="n">ybl</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">y0</span><span class="p">),</span> <span class="n">axis</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">)</span>
        
        <span class="c"># reassign Pinit and y0 for next loop iteration</span>
        <span class="n">Pinit</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">sol</span>
        <span class="n">y0</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">ybl</span>
    
        <span class="k">print</span> <span class="s">&quot;--------------------------------------&quot;</span>


    <span class="c"># End timer</span>
    <span class="n">toc</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">time</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">time</span><span class="p">()</span>
        
    <span class="c"># Output best values    </span>
    <span class="k">print</span> <span class="s">&quot;Best parameters&quot;</span>
    <span class="k">print</span> <span class="n">sol</span>

    <span class="k">print</span> <span class="s">&quot;Initial condition&quot;</span>
    <span class="k">print</span> <span class="n">ybl</span>
    
    <span class="k">print</span> <span class="s">&quot;</span><span class="se">\n</span><span class="s">Time of Execution (hh:mm:ss)&quot;</span>
    <span class="k">print</span> <span class="nb">str</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">datetime</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">timedelta</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">seconds</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="nb">int</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">toc</span> <span class="o">-</span> <span class="n">tic</span><span class="p">)))</span>

    <span class="k">return</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="n">output_prms</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">output_y0</span><span class="p">)</span>
    

<span class="c"># Iterate 20 times exhibits good convergence</span>
<span class="n">iterations</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="mi">20</span>
<span class="n">output_prms</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">output_y0</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">assess</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">Pinit</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">y0</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">ii</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">gi</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">gv</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">iterations</span><span class="p">)</span>
</pre></div>

</div>
</div>

<div class="vbox output_wrapper">
<div class="output vbox">

<h1 id="plot-results-and-error">Plot results and error</h1>
</div>
<div class="cell border-box-sizing code_cell vbox">
<div class="input hbox">
<div class="prompt input_prompt">
In&nbsp;[11]:
</div>
<div class="input_area box-flex1">
<div class="highlight"><pre><span class="c"># get curves with best parameters</span>
<span class="n">sol</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">output_prms</span><span class="p">[:,</span><span class="o">-</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">]</span>
<span class="n">ybl</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">output_y0</span><span class="p">[:,</span><span class="o">-</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">]</span>

<span class="c"># plot data</span>
<span class="n">plt</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">figure</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">)</span>
<span class="n">plt</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">plot</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">t</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">ii</span><span class="p">)</span>

<span class="n">plt</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">figure</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="mi">2</span><span class="p">)</span>
<span class="n">plt</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">plot</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">t</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">gi</span><span class="p">)</span>

<span class="k">for</span> <span class="n">i</span> <span class="ow">in</span> <span class="n">np</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">arange</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">np</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">size</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">gv</span><span class="p">)):</span>
    <span class="n">mp</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">gv</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="n">i</span><span class="p">]</span>

<h1 id="convergence-of-solution-and-initial-condition">Convergence of solution and initial condition</h1>
</div>
<div class="cell border-box-sizing code_cell vbox">
<div class="input hbox">
<div class="prompt input_prompt">
In&nbsp;[12]:
</div>
<div class="input_area box-flex1">
<div class="highlight"><pre><span class="c"># Plot history of output parameters and initial conditions to show convergence</span>

<span class="k">def</span> <span class="nf">show_convergence</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">output_prms</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">output_y0</span><span class="p">):</span>
    <span class="c"># Show convergence of parameters</span>

    <span class="n">plt</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">figure</span><span class="p">()</span>
    <span class="n">plt</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">suptitle</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s">&#39;Parameters&#39;</span><span class="p">)</span>
    <span class="k">for</span> <span class="n">i</span> <span class="ow">in</span> <span class="n">np</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">arange</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="nb">len</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">output_prms</span><span class="p">)):</span>
        <span class="n">plt</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">subplot</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="mi">4</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="mi">4</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="n">i</span><span class="o">+</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">)</span>
        <span class="n">plt</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">plot</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">output_prms</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="n">i</span><span class="p">,:])</span>
        
    <span class="n">plt</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">figure</span><span class="p">()</span>
    <span class="c">#for i in np.arange(len(output_y0)):</span>
    <span class="c">#    plt.subplot(1,7,i+1)</span>
    <span class="c">#    plt.plot(output_y0[i,:])</span>
    <span class="n">plt</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">title</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s">&#39;Initial condition&#39;</span><span class="p">)</span>
    <span class="n">plt</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">plot</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">np</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">transpose</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">output_y0</span><span class="p">))</span>

<span class="n">show_convergence</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">output_prms</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">output_y0</span><span class="p">)</span>
</pre></div>
